This information will not be deemed to be incorporated by reference into any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except to the extent that the Company specifically incorporates it by reference.</p>

<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Exhibit 99.1</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><img src="gignxgcaeoeu000001.jpg" title="" alt="" style="width:226px;height:64px;"></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;;font-size:18pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:18pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">LM Funding Reports Net Income of $11.1 Million or $2.05 Per Basic Common Share for the Second Quarter of 2021</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">TAMPA, FL /&nbsp;&nbsp;August 16, 2021 /&#160;LM Funding America, Inc. (NASDAQ:LMFA) ("LM Funding" or "LMFA"),<font style="font-weight:normal;">&#160;a technology-based specialty finance company, today announced its financial results for the three and six months ended June 30, 2021.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Financial Highlights for the Three and Six Month Period Ended June 30, 2021:</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#1D2228;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#1D2228;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#1D2228;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#1D2228;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Net income attributable to LM Funding for the three and six-month periods ended June 30, 2021 totaled $11.1 million or $2.05 per basic and diluted share and $15.5 million or $2.96 per basic and $2.95 per diluted share, respectively</font>.</p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#1D2228;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#1D2228;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#1D2228;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#1D2228;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Cash increased to $22.2 million or approximately $4.09 per basic and diluted share on June 30, 2021 as compared to $11.6 million on December 31, 2020</font>.</p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#1D2228;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#1D2228;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#1D2228;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#1D2228;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Working capital as of June 30, 2021 was $29.7 million or $5.49 per basic and diluted share</font>.</p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.33%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#auto;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman';text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"></font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:'Times New Roman'">&#8226;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:left;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#auto;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#1D2228;">As of August 6, 2021, there were 5,414,296 common shares outstanding. </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#1D2228;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;We continue to operate under the tagline &#8220;<font style="font-style:italic;">We Buy Problems</font>&#8221;.&nbsp;&nbsp;Bruce M. Rodgers, Chairman and CEO of LM Funding said.&nbsp;&nbsp;&#8220;In the first two quarters, we originated, structured, and monetized our problem-buying business operations to generate $2.96 in net income per basic and diluted share.&nbsp;&nbsp;As our balance sheet has grown our opportunities to buy problems has increased.&nbsp;&nbsp;With a stronger balance sheet, we could also take larger participations in the deals we put together.&nbsp;&nbsp; Although we originated, structured, and executed the two BRQS transactions and recognized $14.1 million in gains this year, we only participated in less than one-third of the principal investment required in these deals and outsourced the balance to third parties.&nbsp;&nbsp;So we plan to continue to combine our team&#8217;s strengths and our balance sheet with $5.49 per share of working capital to buy problems and solve them profitably.&#8221;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;color:#1D2228;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Operational Highlights for the First Six Months of 2021 to Date:</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:6.67%;text-indent:-3.33%;color:#1D2228;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#x2022;<font style="font-family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font><font style="font-family:Calibri;">LMFA announced plans to develop accounting practices and controls for operating with digital assets and has announced plans to purchase up to $2 million in Bitcoin and Ether. </font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:6.67%;text-indent:-3.33%;color:#1D2228;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#x2022;<font style="font-family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font><font style="font-family:Calibri;">LM Funding is developing a digital asset technology strategy to grow its community association receivables business both organically and through acquisitions. </font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:6.67%;text-indent:-3.33%;color:#1D2228;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#x2022;<font style="font-family:Times New Roman;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </font><font style="font-family:Calibri;">LM Funding sponsored a special acquisition company, or SPAC, and closed a $103.5 million upsized IPO (NASDAQ: LMAO). Net investment by LMFA in LMAO totals $6.4 million or approximately $1.17 per LMFA share. </font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &#x2022;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<font style="color:#1D2228;font-family:Calibri;">LMAO is targeting a business combination in the financial services or financial technology sectors</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">About LM Funding America:</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">LM Funding America, Inc., together with its subsidiaries, is a technology-based specialty finance company that provides funding to nonprofit community associations (Associations) primarily located in the state of Florida, as well as in the states of Washington, Colorado and Illinois, by funding a certain portion of the associations' </p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">rights to delinquent accounts that are selected by the Associations arising from unpaid Association assessments.</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-family:Calibri;font-size:12pt;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Forward-Looking Statements:</p>
<p style="margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-style:italic;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">This press release may contain forward-looking statements made pursuant to the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. Words such as &#8220;anticipate,&#8221; &#8220;believe,&#8221; &#8220;estimate,&#8221; &#8220;expect,&#8221; &#8220;intend,&#8221; &#8220;plan,&#8221; and &#8220;project&#8221; and other similar words and expressions are intended to signify forward-looking statements. Forward-looking statements are not guaranties of future results and conditions but rather are subject to various risks and uncertainties. Some of these risks and uncertainties are identified in the company's most recent Annual Report on Form 10-K and its other filings with the SEC, which are available at www.sec.gov. These risks and uncertainties include, without limitation, uncertainty created by the COVID-19 pandemic, our ability to acquire new accounts in our specialty finance business at appropriate prices, the need for capital, our ability to hire and retain new employees, changes in governmental regulations that affect our ability to collected sufficient amounts on defaulted consumer receivables, changes in the credit or capital markets, changes in interest rates, and negative press regarding the debt collection industry.&nbsp;&nbsp;The occurrence of any of these risks and uncertainties could have a material adverse effect on our business, financial condition, and results of operations.</p>
